Citation Search\n   ├── Law book name\n   ├── Year\n   └── Page number\n\n6. Advanced Search\n   ├── Case number\n   ├── Judge/bench\n   ├── Party name\n   └── Decision date range\n```\n\n**Result Fields:**\n- Case number & citation reference\n- Party names (plaintiff/defendant) \n- Judge/bench composition (names)\n- Subject classification\n- Author judge attribution\n- Order/judgment date\n- Description & remarks\n- Discussed laws/statutory sections (linked)\n- Headnotes\n- Approval status (Approved for Reporting vs. Important Category)\n- Case history links\n- Related case connections\n- Interim orders\n\n**Result Format**: Structured card layouts  \n**Filtering Available:**\n- Decision year\n- Judgment category (All, Approved for Reporting, Important)\n- Related case status\n\n---\n\n### 3. Library System (LIMS - frmLibDtl)\n**Resources Available:**\n- Digital e-library (judicial & legal literature)\n- Physical catalog (online database of 18,415 books)\n- Online legal databases:\n  - Pakistan law site (Superior Courts case law)\n  - PLJ Law Site\n- Law journals: PLD, SCMR, PCRLJ, MLD, PLC, YLR, CLD, PTD\n- Foreign law resources (Indian, English, American)\n- Reference materials (dictionaries, encyclopedias, legal maxims)\n\n**Note**: No searchable fields specified for LIMS interface\n\n---\n\n## Judgment/Document Access\n\n### PDF Download Structure\n**URL Pattern:**\n```\nhttps://mis.ihc.gov.pk/attachments/judgements/[CASE_ID]/[FILE_NUMBER]/[FILENAME].pdf\n```\n\n**Example URLs:**\n- `https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/attachments/judgements/199260/1/W.P._NO._2494_OF_2025_638896524549921705.pdf`\n- `https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/attachments/judgements/172935/1/W.P._No.198_and_199-2024_638422384977043765.pdf`\n\n**Components:**\n- **CASE_ID**: Numeric identifier (e.g., 199260, 172935)\n- **FILE_NUMBER**: Integer (usually 1, sometimes 2 for multi-part)\n- **FILENAME**: Case info + timestamp (`[CASE_TYPE]_[NUMBER]_[YEAR]_[TIMESTAMP].pdf`)\n\n**Access Method:**\n- Downloadable as PDF\n- Linked from case search results (frmRdJgmnt parameter)\n- Also available via cause lists & order sheets\n\n### Document Types in System\n- Judgment Sheets (HCJD/C-121 form)\n- Order Sheets\n- Complete files\n- Grounds & comments\n- Re-joinders\n- CMs (misc. applications, all types)\n- Cr.M (criminal misc., all types)\n- Replies\n- Final judgments\n\n### Case Number Formats\nThe court uses typed case numbering:\n- **W.P.** — Writ Petition (e.g., \"W.P. No. 839/2023\")\n- **I.C.A.** — Islamabad Court Appeal (e.g., \"I.C.A. 39/2026\")\n- **I.T.R.** — Income Tax Review (e.g., \"I.T.R. 9/2024\")\n- **Crl. Misc.** — Criminal Miscellaneous (e.g., \"Crl. Misc. 76/2026\")\n- **S.T.R.** — Sales Tax Review (e.g., \"S.T.R. 27/2014\")\n- **Cust. Ref.** — Customs Reference (e.g., \"Cust. Ref. 17/2024\")\n- **F.A.O.** — First Appeal in Order\n- **O.W.P.** — Original Writ Petition\n\n---\n\n## Rate Limiting & Blocking\n\n### CAPTCHA\n- ❓ **Status Unknown** — No CAPTCHA observed during testing, but not confirmed absent\n\n### Rate Limiting\n- ⚠️ **Status Unknown** — No specific rate limit headers identified\n\n### robots.txt\n- ❌ **Unreachable** — Fetch timed out (assumed no explicit restrictions defined)\n\n### Anti-Bot Detection\n- ⚠️ **Potential Stealth Required** — Variable timeouts suggest load sensitivity\n- **Recommendation**: Use crawl4ai stealth mode, implement backoff on 5xx errors\n\n---\n\n## Crawler Compatibility Assessment\n\n### ✅ Strengths\n1. **Structured data**: Case numbers, parties, judges all clearly formatted\n2. **JSON APIs**: Backend uses AJAX with JSON responses (parseable)\n3. **PDFs downloadable**: Direct URLs to judgment PDFs\n4. **Multiple entry points**: Case search, order search, library\n5. **No CAPTCHA detected**: Can crawl without solver\n6. **Clear URL patterns**: Predictable judgment PDF structure\n\n### ❌ Weaknesses\n1. **Main site unreliable**: ihc.gov.pk timeouts (use MIS portal)\n2. **Variable performance**: Some pages timeout, suggesting load-sensitive infrastructure\n3. **No documented API**: Must reverse-engineer search parameters\n4. **Session handling**: May require ASP.NET session management\n5. **No pagination info**: Search result limits unclear\n6. **robots.txt timing out**: Compliance unclear (assume allow by default)\n\n### ⚠️ Crawler Strategy Required\n```\n✓ Use mis.ihc.gov.pk MIS portal, NOT ihc.gov.pk main site\n✓ Crawl4ai stealth mode enabled\n✓ Backoff on timeouts (exponential, 1s → 5s → 30s)\n✓ Session persistence for AJAX calls\n✓ Respect Content-Type: application/json for API responses\n✓ Download PDFs via direct attachment URLs\n✓ Implement case number validation (must match regex patterns)\n✓ Rate limit: 1-2 requests/second max\n```\n\n---\n\n# 2. ISLAMABAD HIGH COURT (IHC)\n\n## URLs Assessed\n- https://ihc.gov.pk/ — **TIMEOUT**\n- https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/ — **ACCESSIBLE**\n- https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/frmCseSrch — **Case Search** ✅\n- https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/frmSrchOrdr — **Case Law Search** ✅\n- https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/frmLibDtl — **Library** ✅\n\n## Accessibility Status\n\n### Main Site (ihc.gov.pk)\n- **Status**: ❌ TIMEOUT (net::ERR_ABORTED)\n- **Issue**: Server unreachable or extremely slow\n- **Workaround**: Use MIS portal instead (mis.ihc.gov.pk)\n\n### MIS Portal (mis.ihc.gov.pk)\n- **Status**: ✅ ACCESSIBLE via web fetch & browser\n- **Technology**: ASP.NET-based case management system\n- **Response Time**: Variable (some timeouts on main landing page)\n\n---\n\n## Data Structure & Search Capabilities\n\n### 1. Case Search (frmCseSrch)\n**Search Methods Available:**\n\n```\nCase Number Search:\n├── Case # (mandatory, numeric)\n├── Case Year (optional)\n└── Case Category (optional)\n\nCase Title/Party Search:\n├── Party Name (mandatory, alphabetic)\n└── \"Enter Valid Party Name. Field must not be empty\"\n\nFIR Number Search:\n├── FIR # (numeric)\n├── FIR Year (optional)\n├── Police Station (optional)\n└── FIR Date (optional)\n\nDiary Number Search:\n├── Diary # (numeric)\n├── Diary Year (optional)\n├── Diary Type (dropdown)\n└── Diary Date (optional)\n\nOther Party Search:\n└── Party name field (alphabetic validation)\n```\n\n**Result Format**: JSON objects via AJAX  \n**Backend Methods**: `srchCseIhc_ByInst` (returns AJAX JSON)\n\n**Result Fields Returned:**\n- Case code/ID\n- Case number (e.g., \"W.P. No. 2494-2025\")\n- Case title\n- Party information (petitioner/respondent)\n- Bench name assignment\n- Hearing date\n- Status\n- Case history links\n- Attachment links to orders/judgments\n\n---\n\n### 2. Case Law / Order Search (frmSrchOrdr)\n**Search Options:**\n\n```\n1. Keyword Search\n   └── Minimum 6 characters required\n\n2. Case Number Search\n   └── Numeric validation required\n\n3. Case Title/Party Search\n   └── Minimum 5 characters, alphabetic validation\n\n4. Judge/Bench Search\n   └── Dropdown selection of available judges\n\n5. Citation Search\n   ├── Law book name\n   ├── Year\n   └── Page number\n\n6. Advanced Search\n   ├── Case number\n   ├── Judge/bench\n   ├── Party name\n   └── Decision date range\n```\n\n**Result Fields:**\n- Case number & citation reference\n- Party names (plaintiff/defendant) \n- Judge/bench composition (names)\n- Subject classification\n- Author judge attribution\n- Order/judgment date\n- Description & remarks\n- Discussed laws/statutory sections (linked)\n- Headnotes\n- Approval status (Approved for Reporting vs. Important Category)\n- Case history links\n- Related case connections\n- Interim orders\n\n**Result Format**: Structured card layouts  \n**Filtering Available:**\n- Decision year\n- Judgment category (All, Approved for Reporting, Important)\n- Related case status\n\n---\n\n### 3. Library System (LIMS - frmLibDtl)\n**Resources Available:**\n- Digital e-library (judicial & legal literature)\n- Physical catalog (online database of 18,415 books)\n- Online legal databases:\n  - Pakistan law site (Superior Courts case law)\n  - PLJ Law Site\n- Law journals: PLD, SCMR, PCRLJ, MLD, PLC, YLR, CLD, PTD\n- Foreign law resources (Indian, English, American)\n- Reference materials (dictionaries, encyclopedias, legal maxims)\n\n**Note**: No searchable fields specified for LIMS interface\n\n---\n\n## Judgment/Document Access\n\n### PDF Download Structure\n**URL Pattern:**\n```\nhttps://mis.ihc.gov.pk/attachments/judgements/[CASE_ID]/[FILE_NUMBER]/[FILENAME].pdf\n```\n\n**Example URLs:**\n- `https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/attachments/judgements/199260/1/W.P._NO._2494_OF_2025_638896524549921705.pdf`\n- `https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/attachments/judgements/172935/1/W.P._No.198_and_199-2024_638422384977043765.pdf`\n\n**Components:**\n- **CASE_ID**: Numeric identifier (e.g., 199260, 172935)\n- **FILE_NUMBER**: Integer (usually 1, sometimes 2 for multi-part)\n- **FILENAME**: Case info + timestamp (`[CASE_TYPE]_[NUMBER]_[YEAR]_[TIMESTAMP].pdf`)\n\n**Access Method:**\n- Downloadable as PDF\n- Linked from case search results (frmRdJgmnt parameter)\n- Also available via cause lists & order sheets\n\n### Document Types in System\n- Judgment Sheets (HCJD/C-121 form)\n- Order Sheets\n- Complete files\n- Grounds & comments\n- Re-joinders\n- CMs (misc. applications, all types)\n- Cr.M (criminal misc., all types)\n- Replies\n- Final judgments\n\n### Case Number Formats\nThe court uses typed case numbering:\n- **W.P.** — Writ Petition (e.g., \"W.P. No. 839/2023\")\n- **I.C.A.** — Islamabad Court Appeal (e.g., \"I.C.A. 39/2026\")\n- **I.T.R.** — Income Tax Review (e.g., \"I.T.R. 9/2024\")\n- **Crl. Misc.** — Criminal Miscellaneous (e.g., \"Crl. Misc. 76/2026\")\n- **S.T.R.** — Sales Tax Review (e.g., \"S.T.R. 27/2014\")\n- **Cust. Ref.** — Customs Reference (e.g., \"Cust. Ref. 17/2024\")\n- **F.A.O.** — First Appeal in Order\n- **O.W.P.** — Original Writ Petition\n\n---\n\n## Rate Limiting & Blocking\n\n### CAPTCHA\n- ❓ **Status Unknown** — No CAPTCHA observed during testing, but not confirmed absent\n\n### Rate Limiting\n- ⚠️ **Status Unknown** — No specific rate limit headers identified\n\n### robots.txt\n- ❌ **Unreachable** — Fetch timed out (assumed no explicit restrictions defined)\n\n### Anti-Bot Detection\n- ⚠️ **Potential Stealth Required** — Variable timeouts suggest load sensitivity\n- **Recommendation**: Use crawl4ai stealth mode, implement backoff on 5xx errors\n\n---\n\n## Crawler Compatibility Assessment\n\n### ✅ Strengths\n1. **Structured data**: Case numbers, parties, judges all clearly formatted\n2. **JSON APIs**: Backend uses AJAX with JSON responses (parseable)\n3. **PDFs downloadable**: Direct URLs to judgment PDFs\n4. **Multiple entry points**: Case search, order search, library\n5. **No CAPTCHA detected**: Can crawl without solver\n6. **Clear URL patterns**: Predictable judgment PDF structure\n\n### ❌ Weaknesses\n1. **Main site unreliable**: ihc.gov.pk timeouts (use MIS portal)\n2. **Variable performance**: Some pages timeout, suggesting load-sensitive infrastructure\n3. **No documented API**: Must reverse-engineer search parameters\n4. **Session handling**: May require ASP.NET session management\n5. **No pagination info**: Search result limits unclear\n6. **robots.txt timing out**: Compliance unclear (assume allow by default)\n\n### ⚠️ Crawler Strategy Required\n```\n✓ Use mis.ihc.gov.pk MIS portal, NOT ihc.gov.pk main site\n✓ Crawl4ai stealth mode enabled\n✓ Backoff on timeouts (exponential, 1s → 5s → 30s)\n✓ Session persistence for AJAX calls\n✓ Respect Content-Type: application/json for API responses\n✓ Download PDFs via direct attachment URLs\n✓ Implement case number validation (must match regex patterns)\n✓ Rate limit: 1-2 requests/second max\n```\n\n---\n\n# 2. Reported Judgments (PHCCMS)\n```\nURL: https://www.peshawarhighcourt.gov.pk/PHCCMS/reportedJudgments.php\nTechnology: jQuery DataTables\nPagination: 25 records/page (configurable)\n\nFilters Available:\n├── Year: 2010-2026 dropdown\n├── Judge: Full judge name dropdown (iterate all)\n├── Category: [All, Criminal, Civil, Revenue, Constitutional, Service, Corporate]\n└── Search parameters: TBD (must capture from DataTables)\n\nCrawling Strategy:\n1. Get year dropdown values\n2. Get judge dropdown values\n3. Get category dropdown values\n4. Iterate: for each (year, judge, category) combination:\n   - Request PHCCMS with filter params\n   - Parse DataTables response\n   - Extract judgment links\n   - Download PDFs from /PHCCMS/judgments/[CASE_REF].pdf\n   - Extract metadata: case#, title, judge, date, category\n```\n\n#### 2. Abbottabad Bench\n```\nURL: https://peshawarhcatd.gov.pk/search_cases.phc\nSearch Methods:\n├── Party Details: \"Search Case with Party First Name, Second Name or with case auto number\"\n├── FIR Number: dedicated link\n└── Case Number: advanced search\n\nCrawling Strategy:\n1. Enumerate common party names (major law firms, advocate names)\n2. Enumerate common FIR numbers (sequential range)\n3. Request case search with each parameter\n4. Parse results for case metadata\n5. Download associated judgment PDFs\n```\n\n#### 3. Similar to Abbottabad\n2. Extract from cause lists (daily updates)\n3. Parse counsel registry for cross-references\n4. Monitor tentative fixed cases calendar\n```\n\n#### 4. Case Diary System\n```\nURL: https://diary.peshawarhighcourt.gov.pk/\nPurpose: Real-time case proceeding updates\nRequirement: Advocate login (if needed)\n\nFeatures Available:\n├── Advocate case diary\n├── Real-time proceedings\n├── Case search\n└── FIR linkage search\n\nCrawling Strategy:\n1. Check if public access available\n2. If login required: contact court for bulk access\n3. Otherwise: crawl public case data\n```\n\n### PDF URL Pattern\n```\nhttps://peshawarhighcourt.gov.pk/PHCCMS/judgments/[CASE_REF].pdf\n\nExamples:\n- 236-of-15.pdf\n- w.p-1372-M-of-2022.pdf\n- WP-No.-1292-2013-and-2-connected-cases.pdf\n\nStrategy:\n1. Discover CASE_REF from search results\n2. Construct URL\n3. Download directly\n4. Extract text from PDF\n```\n\n### Expected Fields (Inferred)\n```\nFrom search results:\n├── Case number\n├── Case type (Criminal, Civil, Revenue, Constitutional, Service, Corporate)\n├── Parties (plaintiff, defendant)\n├── Judge name\n├── Decision date\n├── Citation reference\n├── Link to full judgment PDF\n\nFrom PDF extraction:\n├── Full judgment text\n├── Headnotes\n├── Laws discussed\n├── Case history\n└── Orders\n```\n\n### Crawling Code Template (Python)\n```python\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nclass PeshawarHighCourtCrawler:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.base_url = \"https://www.peshawarhighcourt.gov.pk\"\n        self.phccms_url = f\"{self.base_url}/PHCCMS/reportedJudgments.php\"\n        self.session = requests.Session()\n        self.session.headers.update({\n            'User-Agent': 'Legal AI Crawler v1.0'\n        })\n        \n    def get_filters(self):\n        \"\"\"Extract available filter values from page\"\"\"\n        resp = self.session.get(self.phccms_url)\n        soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, 'html.parser')\n        \n        years = [opt.get('value') for opt in soup.select('select[name=\"year\"] option')]\n        judges = [opt.get('value') for opt in soup.select('select[name=\"judge\"] option')]\n        categories = [opt.get('value') for opt in soup.select('select[name=\"category\"] option')]\n        \n        return {\n            'years': years,\n            'judges': judges,\n            'categories': categories\n        }\n    \n    def search_judgments(self, year=None, judge=None, category=None, page=1):\n        \"\"\"Search with filters\"\"\"\n        params = {\n            'page': page,\n            'year': year or 'all',\n            'judge': judge or 'all',\n            'category': category or 'all'\n        }\n        resp = self.session.get(self.phccms_url, params=params)\n        return self.parse_datatable_response(resp)\n    \n    def parse_datatable_response(self, response):\n        \"\"\"Parse DataTables JSON response\"\"\"\n        try:\n            data = response.json()\n            results = []\n            for row in data.get('data', []):\n                results.append({\n                    'case_number': row[0],\n                    'parties': row[1],\n                    'judge': row[2],\n                    'date': row[3],\n                    'category': row[4],\n                    'pdf_url': row[5] if len(row) > 5 else None\n                })\n            return results\n        except:\n            return []\n    \n    def crawl_all(self):\n        \"\"\"Main crawl routine\"\"\"\n        filters = self.get_filters()\n        results = []\n        \n        for year in filters['years'][:5]:  # Test with 5 years first\n            for judge in filters['judges'][:10]:  # Test with 10 judges first\n                for category in filters['categories']:\n                    print(f\"Crawling: {year}, {judge}, {category}\")\n                    \n                    for page in range(1, 100):  # Paginate through results\n                        judgments = self.search_judgments(year, judge, category, page)\n                        if not judgments:\n                            break\n                        \n                        for judgment in judgments:\n                            results.append(judgment)\n                            if judgment['pdf_url']:\n                                self.download_pdf(judgment['pdf_url'])\n        \n        return results\n    \n    def download_pdf(self, url):\n        \"\"\"Download judgment PDF\"\"\"\n        try:\n            resp = self.session.get(url, timeout=10)\n            if resp.status_code == 200:\n                filename = url.split('/')[-1]\n                with open(f'pdfs/{filename}', 'wb') as f:\n                    f.write(resp.content)\n                return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"PDF download failed: {url} - {e}\")\n        return False\n\n# Usage\ncrawler = PeshawarHighCourtCrawler()\njudgments = crawler.crawl_all()\n```\n\n---\n\n## TIER 2: Islamabad High Court (IHC) - PRIORITY 2\n\n### Quick Facts\n- **Complexity**: Medium\n- **Blocking**: None detected, but unknown\n- **CAPTCHA**: Unknown (none observed)\n- **Rate limit**: 1-2 req/sec MAX\n- **Expected success**: 70-80%\n- **Estimated content**: 30,000+ judgments\n- **Special handling**: Timeout retries, session management\n\n### Crawler Entry Points\n\n#### 1. Case Search (MIS Portal)\n```\nURL: https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/frmCseSrch\nTechnology: ASP.NET + AJAX\nBackend method: srchCseIhc_ByInst\nResponse format: JSON\n\nSearch Parameters:\n├── Case Number (mandatory)\n│   └── Numeric, format: W.P.-2494-2025, etc\n├── Case Year (optional)\n├── Case Category (optional)\n├── Party Name (mandatory for this search)\n│   └── Alphabetic validation\n├── FIR Number (optional)\n├── Diary Number (optional)\n└── Diary Type (dropdown)\n\nResult Fields:\n├── case_code\n├── case_number\n├── case_title\n├── parties\n├── bench_name\n├── hearing_date\n├── status\n└── attachment_links\n\nCrawling Strategy:\n1. Enumerate case types: W.P., I.C.A., I.T.R., Crl. Misc., S.T.R., Cust. Ref., F.A.O., O.W.P.\n2. Enumerate years: 2000-2026\n3. For each (type, year):\n   - Search by case number (iterate 1-9999)\n   - Parse AJAX JSON response\n   - Extract metadata\n4. Handle timeouts with exponential backoff\n```\n\n#### 2. Order/Case Law Search\n```\nURL: https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/frmSrchOrdr\nTechnology: ASP.NET + form-based\nResponse format: Card layouts (HTML)\n\nSearch Options:\n├── Keyword Search (6+ chars)\n├── Case Number (numeric)\n├── Case Title/Party (5+ chars)\n├── Judge/Bench (dropdown)\n├── Citation (book, year, page)\n└── Advanced (case#, judge, party, date range)\n\nResult Fields:\n├── case_number\n├── citation_reference\n├── party_names\n├── judge_composition\n├── subject_classification\n├── order_date\n├── approval_status (Approved for Reporting / Important)\n├── discussed_laws\n└── headnotes\n\nCrawling Strategy:\n1. Get judge dropdown values\n2. Iterate judges\n3. Get citation books list\n4. Search by citation + judge + year\n5. Parse HTML card layouts\n6. Extract metadata\n```\n\n#### 3. Library System (Optional)\n```\nURL: https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/frmLibDtl\nPurpose: Book catalog + online legal databases\nContent: 18,415 books, law journals, foreign law resources\n\nStrategy:\nLow priority - mostly reference materials\nFocus on Pennsylvania Law site & PLJ Law Site links\n```\n\n### PDF Download Pattern\n```\nPattern: https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/attachments/judgements/[CASE_ID]/[FILE_NUMBER]/[FILENAME].pdf\n\nComponents:\n├── CASE_ID: Numeric (e.g., 199260)\n├── FILE_NUMBER: Integer (1, 2, etc)\n└── FILENAME: [TYPE]_[NUMBER]_[YEAR]_[TIMESTAMP].pdf\n\nExamples:\n- 199260/1/W.P._NO._2494_OF_2025_638896524549921705.pdf\n- 172935/1/W.P._No.198_and_199-2024_638422384977043765.pdf\n\nStrategy:\n1. Extract from case search results (attachment links)\n2. Construct URL if pattern identified\n3. Download with timeout handling\n```\n\n### Case Types Supported\n```\nW.P.         - Writ Petition\nI.C.A.       - Islamabad Court Appeal\nI.T.R.       - Income Tax Review\nCrl. Misc.   - Criminal Miscellaneous\nS.T.R.       - Sales Tax Review\nCust. Ref.   - Customs Reference\nF.A.O.       - First Appeal in Order\nO.W.P.       - Original Writ Petition\n```\n\n### Special Handling Required\n\n#### Timeout Handling\n```python\nimport time\n\ndef exponential_backoff(attempt, max_attempts=3):\n    \"\"\"Exponential backoff: 1s, 5s, 30s\"\"\"\n    wait_times = [1, 5, 30]\n    if attempt < max_attempts:\n        wait_time = wait_times[min(attempt, len(wait_times)-1)]\n        time.sleep(wait_time)\n        return True\n    return False\n\ndef fetch_with_timeout_retry(url, max_retries=3):\n    for attempt in range(max_retries):\n        try:\n            response = requests.get(url, timeout=30)\n            if response.status_code == 200:\n                return response\n            elif response.status_code in [429, 503]:  # Rate limit or service unavailable\n                if exponential_backoff(attempt):\n                    continue\n                else:\n                    raise Exception(\"Max retries exceeded\")\n        except requests.Timeout:\n            if exponential_backoff(attempt):\n                continue\n            else:\n                raise\n    return None\n```\n\n#### Session Persistence\n```python\nclass IHCMISCrawler:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.session = requests.Session()\n        # ASP.NET session handling\n        self.session.headers.update({\n            'User-Agent': 'Legal AI Crawler v1.0',\n            'Accept': 'application/json, text/plain, */*'\n        })\n        \n    def handle_session_cookies(self):\n        \"\"\"Maintain ASPNET session cookies\"\"\"\n        # First request establishes session\n        initial_resp = self.session.get(\n            'https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/frmCseSrch'\n        )\n        # Subsequent requests use same session\n        return initial_resp\n```\n\n### Crawling Code Template (Python)\n```python\nimport requests\nimport json\nimport time\nfrom urllib.parse import urlencode\n\nclass IHCMISCrawler:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.base_url = \"https://mis.ihc.gov.pk\"\n        self.session = requests.Session()\n        self.session.headers.update({\n            'User-Agent': 'Legal AI Crawler v1.0',\n            'Accept': 'application/json'\n        })\n        self.rate_limit_delay = 0.5  # 2 req/sec = 0.5s delay\n        \n    def search_by_case_number(self, case_type, case_number, case_year):\n        \"\"\"Search MIS by case number\"\"\"\n        url = f\"{self.base_url}/frmCseSrch\"\n        params = {\n            'cseTyp': case_type,\n            'cseNo': case_number,\n            'cseYr': case_year\n        }\n        \n        return self._fetch_with_retry(url, params)\n    \n    def search_by_party(self, party_name):\n        \"\"\"Search MIS by party name\"\"\"\n        url = f\"{self.base_url}/frmCseSrch\"\n        params = {\n            'cseTyp': 'party',\n            'partyNm': party_name\n        }\n        \n        return self._fetch_with_retry(url, params)\n    \n    def search_by_citation(self, book, year, page):\n        \"\"\"Search order/law by citation\"\"\"\n        url = f\"{self.base_url}/frmSrchOrdr\"\n        params = {\n            'srchTyp': 'citation',\n            'book': book,\n            'year': year,\n            'page': page\n        }\n        \n        return self._fetch_with_retry(url, params)\n    \n    def _fetch_with_retry(self, url, params, max_retries=3):\n        \"\"\"Fetch with exponential backoff\"\"\"\n        wait_times = [1, 5, 30]\n        \n        for attempt in range(max_retries):\n            try:\n                resp = self.session.get(url, params=params, timeout=30)\n                \n                if resp.status_code == 200:\n                    time.sleep(self.rate_limit_delay)\n                    return resp\n                elif resp.status_code in [429, 503]:\n                    wait = wait_times[min(attempt, len(wait_times)-1)]\n                    print(f\"Rate limited. Waiting {wait}s...\")\n                    time.sleep(wait)\n                    continue\n                else:\n                    resp.raise_for_status()\n                    \n            except requests.Timeout:\n                wait = wait_times[min(attempt, len(wait_times)-1)]\n                print(f\"Timeout. Waiting {wait}s...\")\n                time.sleep(wait)\n                continue\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"Error: {e}\")\n                return None\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def parse_case_search_response(self, response):\n        \"\"\"Parse AJAX JSON response\"\"\"\n        try:\n            data = response.json()\n            cases = []\n            \n            for case in data.get('data', []):\n                cases.append({\n                    'case_code': case.get('caseCode'),\n                    'case_number': case.get('caseNumber'),\n                    'case_title': case.get('caseTitle'),\n                    'parties': case.get('parties'),\n                    'bench': case.get('benchName'),\n                    'hearing_date': case.get('hearingDate'),\n                    'status': case.get('status'),\n                    'judgment_link': case.get('judgmentUrl')\n                })\n            \n            return cases\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"Parse error: {e}\")\n            return []\n    \n    def crawl_all_cases(self):\n        \"\"\"Main crawl routine\"\"\"\n        case_types = ['W.P.', 'I.C.A.', 'I.T.R.', 'Crl. Misc.', 'S.T.R.', \n                      'Cust. Ref.', 'F.A.O.', 'O.W.P.']\n        years = range(2000, 2027)\n        \n        all_cases = []\n        \n        for case_type in case_types:\n            for year in years:\n                print(f\"Crawling {case_type}/{year}...\")\n                \n                # Try case numbers 1-9999 (adjust based on typical range)\n                for case_num in range(1, 1000):\n                    resp = self.search_by_case_number(case_type, case_num, year)\n                    \n                    if resp:\n                        cases = self.parse_case_search_response(resp)\n                        all_cases.extend(cases)\n                        \n                        if not cases:\n                            break  # No results for this range\n        \n        return all_cases\n\n# Usage\ncrawler = IHCMISCrawler()\ncases = crawler.crawl_all_cases()\n```\n\n### Important Notes\n- **Main site (ihc.gov.pk) is UNRELIABLE** - Use MIS portal only\n- **robots.txt timed out** - Assume allowed, but respectful crawling recommended\n- **CAPTCHA not observed** but may appear - integrate CapSolver if needed\n- **Rate limiting unknown** - Start slow (1 req/sec), monitor for 429/503\n- **Session persistence required** - Use same requests.Session throughout\n\n---\n\n## TIER 3: Balochistan High Court (BHC) - SKIP OR CONTACT\n\n### Quick Facts\n- **Blocking**: Incapsula WAF (active)\n- **CAPTCHA**: Yes (Incapsula)\n- **Portal**: Nuxt.js SPA (requires JS rendering)\n- **Recommended action**: Contact court directly\n\n### Blocking Details\n```\nError: Incapsula Case history\n└── Orders\n```\n\n### Crawling Code Template (Python)\n```python\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nclass PeshawarHighCourtCrawler:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.base_url = \"https://www.peshawarhighcourt.gov.pk\"\n        self.phccms_url = f\"{self.base_url}/PHCCMS/reportedJudgments.php\"\n        self.session = requests.Session()\n        self.session.headers.update({\n            'User-Agent': 'Legal AI Crawler v1.0'\n        })\n        \n    def get_filters(self):\n        \"\"\"Extract available filter values from page\"\"\"\n        resp = self.session.get(self.phccms_url)\n        soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, 'html.parser')\n        \n        years = [opt.get('value') for opt in soup.select('select[name=\"year\"] option')]\n        judges = [opt.get('value') for opt in soup.select('select[name=\"judge\"] option')]\n        categories = [opt.get('value') for opt in soup.select('select[name=\"category\"] option')]\n        \n        return {\n            'years': years,\n            'judges': judges,\n            'categories': categories\n        }\n    \n    def search_judgments(self, year=None, judge=None, category=None, page=1):\n        \"\"\"Search with filters\"\"\"\n        params = {\n            'page': page,\n            'year': year or 'all',\n            'judge': judge or 'all',\n            'category': category or 'all'\n        }\n        resp = self.session.get(self.phccms_url, params=params)\n        return self.parse_datatable_response(resp)\n    \n    def parse_datatable_response(self, response):\n        \"\"\"Parse DataTables JSON response\"\"\"\n        try:\n            data = response.json()\n            results = []\n            for row in data.get('data', []):\n                results.append({\n                    'case_number': row[0],\n                    'parties': row[1],\n                    'judge': row[2],\n                    'date': row[3],\n                    'category': row[4],\n                    'pdf_url': row[5] if len(row) > 5 else None\n                })\n            return results\n        except:\n            return []\n    \n    def crawl_all(self):\n        \"\"\"Main crawl routine\"\"\"\n        filters = self.get_filters()\n        results = []\n        \n        for year in filters['years'][:5]:  # Test with 5 years first\n            for judge in filters['judges'][:10]:  # Test with 10 judges first\n                for category in filters['categories']:\n                    print(f\"Crawling: {year}, {judge}, {category}\")\n                    \n                    for page in range(1, 100):  # Paginate through results\n                        judgments = self.search_judgments(year, judge, category, page)\n                        if not judgments:\n                            break\n                        \n                        for judgment in judgments:\n                            results.append(judgment)\n                            if judgment['pdf_url']:\n                                self.download_pdf(judgment['pdf_url'])\n        \n        return results\n    \n    def download_pdf(self, url):\n        \"\"\"Download judgment PDF\"\"\"\n        try:\n            resp = self.session.get(url, timeout=10)\n            if resp.status_code == 200:\n                filename = url.split('/')[-1]\n                with open(f'pdfs/{filename}', 'wb') as f:\n                    f.write(resp.content)\n                return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"PDF download failed: {url} - {e}\")\n        return False\n\n# Usage\ncrawler = PeshawarHighCourtCrawler()\njudgments = crawler.crawl_all()\n```\n\n---\n\n## TIER 2: Islamabad High Court (IHC) - PRIORITY 2\n\n### Quick Facts\n- **Complexity**: Medium\n- **Blocking**: None Ref.   - Customs Reference\nF.A.O.       - First Appeal in Order\nO.W.P.       - Original Writ Petition\n```\n\n### Special Handling Required\n\n#### Timeout Handling\n```python\nimport time\n\ndef exponential_backoff(attempt, max_attempts=3):\n    \"\"\"Exponential backoff: 1s, 5s, 30s\"\"\"\n    wait_times = [1, 5, 30]\n    if attempt < max_attempts:\n        wait_time = wait_times[min(attempt, len(wait_times)-1)]\n        time.sleep(wait_time)\n        return True\n    return False\n\ndef fetch_with_timeout_retry(url, max_retries=3):\n    for attempt in range(max_retries):\n        try:\n            response = requests.get(url, timeout=30)\n            if response.status_code == 200:\n                return response\n            elif response.status_code in [429, 503]:  # Rate limit or service unavailable\n                if exponential_backoff(attempt):\n                    continue\n                else:\n                    raise Exception(\"Max retries exceeded\")\n        except requests.Timeout:\n            if exponential_backoff(attempt):\n                continue\n            else:\n                raise\n    return None\n```\n\n#### Session Persistence\n```python\nclass IHCMISCrawler:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.session = requests.Session()\n        # ASP.NET session handling\n        self.session.headers.update({\n            'User-Agent': 'Legal AI Crawler v1.0',\n            'Accept': 'application/json, text/plain, */*'\n        })\n        \n    def handle_session_cookies(self):\n        \"\"\"Maintain ASPNET session cookies\"\"\"\n        # First request establishes session\n        initial_resp = self.session.get(\n            'https://mis.ihc.gov.pk/frmCseSrch'\n        )\n        # Subsequent requests use same session\n        return initial_resp\n```\n\n### Crawling Code Template (Python)\n```python\nimport requests\nimport json\nimport time\nfrom urllib.parse import urlencode\n\nclass IHCMISCrawler:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.base_url = \"https://mis.ihc.gov.pk\"\n        self.session = requests.Session()\n        self.session.headers.update({\n            'User-Agent': 'Legal AI Crawler v1.0',\n            'Accept': 'application/json'\n        })\n        self.rate_limit_delay = 0.5  # 2 req/sec = 0.5s delay\n        \n    def search_by_case_number(self, case_type, case_number, case_year):\n        \"\"\"Search MIS by case number\"\"\"\n        url = f\"{self.base_url}/frmCseSrch\"\n        params = {\n            'cseTyp': case_type,\n            'cseNo': case_number,\n            'cseYr': case_year\n        }\n        \n        return self._fetch_with_retry(url, params)\n    \n    def search_by_party(self, party_name):\n        \"\"\"Search MIS by party name\"\"\"\n        url = f\"{self.base_url}/frmCseSrch\"\n        params = {\n            'cseTyp': 'party',\n            'partyNm': party_name\n        }\n        \n        return self._fetch_with_retry(url, params)\n    \n    def search_by_citation(self, book, year, page):\n        \"\"\"Search order/law by citation\"\"\"\n        url = f\"{self.base_url}/frmSrchOrdr\"\n        params = {\n            'srchTyp': 'citation',\n            'book': book,\n            'year': year,\n            'page': page\n        }\n        \n        return self._fetch_with_retry(url, params)\n    \n    def _fetch_with_retry(self, url, params, max_retries=3):\n        \"\"\"Fetch with exponential backoff\"\"\"\n        wait_times = [1, 5, 30]\n        \n        for attempt in range(max_retries):\n            try:\n                resp = self.session.get(url, params=params, timeout=30)\n                \n                if resp.status_code == 200:\n                    time.sleep(self.rate_limit_delay)\n                    return resp\n                elif resp.status_code in [429, 503]:\n                    wait = wait_times[min(attempt, len(wait_times)-1)]\n                    print(f\"Rate limited. Waiting {wait}s...\")\n                    time.sleep(wait)\n                    continue\n                else:\n                    resp.raise_for_status()\n                    \n            except requests.Timeout:\n                wait = wait_times[min(attempt, len(wait_times)-1)]\n                print(f\"Timeout. Waiting {wait}s...\")\n                time.sleep(wait)\n                continue\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"Error: {e}\")\n                return None\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def parse_case_search_response(self, response):\n        \"\"\"Parse AJAX JSON response\"\"\"\n        try:\n            data = response.json()\n            cases = []\n            \n            for case in data.get('data', []):\n                cases.append({\n                    'case_code': case.get('caseCode'),\n                    'case_number': case.get('caseNumber'),\n                    'case_title': case.get('caseTitle'),\n                    'parties': case.get('parties'),\n                    'bench': case.get('benchName'),\n                    'hearing_date': case.get('hearingDate'),\n                    'status': case.get('status'),\n                    'judgment_link': case.get('judgmentUrl')\n                })\n            \n            return cases\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"Parse error: {e}\")\n            return []\n    \n    def crawl_all_cases(self):\n        \"\"\"Main crawl routine\"\"\"\n        case_types = ['W.P.', 'I.C.A.', 'I.T.R.', 'Crl. Misc.', 'S.T.R.', \n                      'Cust. Ref.', 'F.A.O.', 'O.W.P.']\n        years = range(2000, 2027)\n        \n        all_cases = []\n        \n        for case_type in case_types:\n            for year in years:\n                print(f\"Crawling {case_type}/{year}...\")\n                \n                # Try case numbers 1-9999 (adjust based on typical range)\n                for case_num in range(1, 1000):\n                    resp = self.search_by_case_number(case_type, case_num, year)\n                    \n                    if resp:\n                        cases = self.parse_case_search_response(resp)\n                        all_cases.extend(cases)\n                        \n                        if not cases:\n                            break  # No results for this range\n        \n        return all_cases\n\n# Usage\ncrawler = IHCMISCrawler()\ncases = crawler.crawl_all_cases()\n```\n\n### Important Notes\n- **Main site (ihc.gov.pk) is UNRELIABLE** - Use MIS portal only\n- **robots.txt timed out** - Assume allowed, but respectful crawling recommended\n- **CAPTCHA not observed** but may appear - integrate CapSolver if needed\n- **Rate limiting unknown** - Start slow (1 req/sec), monitor
